 More than ten years have passed since this conference, but no information about action on its recommendations is available
 dow najma ne kaha ki samprag sarkaar ke pichley das saal ke kaarykaal main sthiti or kharaab hui he
 On the question of the UPA government holding the opposition responsible for not allowing Parliament to function, he said that the opposition also has as much accountability to the public as the government
 dow najma kaa kahana tha ki vipaksh to mudde uthayega hi, yah to sarkaar ko rasta nikaalnaa he ki kis prakaar vipaksh apane mudde bhi uthaae or sansad kii kaarywahi bhi chalati rahe
 It is also important to note here that standing committees of different departments were formed in 1993
 uske baad se sansad vidheyakon ko vishleshan ke liye in samitiyon ko bhej detii he
 This work goes on throughout the year outside the scheduled meetings of Parliament
 isse bhi sansad kaa kuch kaamkaaj kam hone se baithkon kii sankhya main kami aayi he
 According to information received from the Lok Sabha Secretariat, in the 1950s the average sitting of Lok Sabha was 127 days and Rajya Sabha meeting was 93 days
 lekin ab varsh 2011 ke aankaden dikhaate hai ki donon hi sadanon main yah ausat ghatakar 73 din kaa ho gaya he
 The last few decades have also seen a decline in the number of Bills passed by Parliament
 pehali loksabhaa main 1950 se 1955 ke paanch saal ke dauraan ausatan prativarsh 72 vidheyak paarit kiye gaye lekin 15veen loksabhaa main yah aankada kam hokar 40 tak aa gaya he
 Statistics show that in 1976 Parliament passed the highest record 118 Bills in any one year
 iske mukaable varsh 2004 main sabase kam yani keval 18 vidheyak sansad ne paarit kiye
 According to data provided by PRS Legislative Research, the Parliament's proceedings in the 15th Lok Sabha were frequently interrupted
 varsh 2011 main sheet satr kii samaapti tak 15veen loksabhaa ne uplabdh samay main se keval 70 fisadi samay kaa istemaal kiya jo pichley 25 saal ke sansadeey itihaas main sabase kam he
 The comments pichley do dashak main 1998, 2004 or 2008 main sarvaadhik kam baithken hui or in vashare main baithkon kii sankhya 45 se bhi kam rahi
 Since the first Lok Sabha (1952 to 1957) there has been a period of decline in Lok Sabha meetings
 pehali loksabhaa ke dauraan paanch saal kii avadhi main 677 baithken (3784 ghante) hui jo ek ricard he
 There were 565 meetings of the Rajya Sabha during the same period
 1971 se 1977 ke dauraan loksabhaa ne 4071 ghante yani 613 baithkon main kaam kiya
 In 1956, there were 151 and 113 meetings of the Lok Sabha and Rajya Sabha respectively, which is the record for the most meetings till date
 varsh 2006 tak aate aate sansad kii baithkon kii sankhya 77 tak simat gai or varsh 2007 main yah or kam hokar 66 din par aa gai
 In this regard, in the All India Conference of Presiding Officers, Chief Ministers, Ministers of Parliamentary Affairs, Leaders of the Party and Whip in 2001, a call was made to take steps to ensure at least 110 meetings of Parliament every year
 sammelan main sifarish kii gai thi ki yadi jaruri ho to samvidhan main sanshodhan ke jariye yah badlaav sunishchit kiya jaae
 Senior member of the Inter Parliamentary Union (IPU) from 1995 to 1999 and President of the Council of IPU from 1999 to 2002, Senior Leader Dr
 Najma Heptulla said in conversation that the declining number of Parliament meetings was a matter of grave concern The recommendations of the conference are dusting the Parliament Library and the government has not taken any initiative in this direction
 is sammelan ko das saal se adhik kaa samay biit chukaa he lekin isaki siforeeshon par karrwai ke bare main koi jaankaree uplabdh nahin he
 Dr
 Najma said that the situation has worsened in the last ten years of the UPA government

 Dr
 Najma said that even if the opposition will raise issues, it is up to the government to find a way how the opposition should raise its issues and the proceedings of Parliament should also continue

 to aise main ek parivaar ke ek hi vyakti ko karj maafee ke liye anumati dena thik nahin he

 rajya sarkaar dwaara yani pati-patni donon kaa milakar sirf dedh lakh ke karj maafee kii anumati di gai thi
 He said that the farmers were told by the government that if the amount of the loan of both is one lakh seventy thousand, then the farmer has to fill the amount above one and a half lakh
 isliye rajya sarkaar dwaara banaai gai upasmiti ke saamne ye maamla charchaa ke liye aayaa
 After a recommendation from the subcommittee in this matter, the cabinet has approved that every person of the farmer family can now apply for loan waiver
 subhash deshmukh ne 'ajtak' ko bataaya ki pati ne 90 hajaar or patni ne 90 hajaar kaa karja agar bank se liya he to dononkarj maafeeka upbhog le paaenge

 subhash dekhmukh ne bataaya ki ab tak 89 lakh kisaanon ne karj maafee ke liye arji di thi

 yah pehali baar he jab rohingya pravaasiyon ko bharat se myanmar bheja jayega

 kachaar jile ke adhikariyon ne bataaya ki jinhen waapas bheja jayega unamem mohammad jamaal, mohabul khan, jamaal hossain, mohammad unuus, sabir ahamed, rahim uddin or mohammad salaam shaamil hai
 Their age is between 26 and 32 years
 bharat sarkaar ne pichley saal sansad ko bataaya tha ki sanyukt raashtra sharnaarthi agency yuanechasiaar main panjikrut 14,000 se adhik rohingya bharat main rahete hai
 However, the aid agencies have reported the number of Rohingya people living in the country at around 40,000
 rakhin rajya main myamar sena ke kathith abhiyaan ke baad rohingya log apni jaan bachaane ke liye ghar chhodkar bhaage the
 The United Nations describes the Rohingya community as the most repressed minority
 maanavadhikaar samooh ‘emnesti international’ ne rohingya logon kii durdasha liye ang saan su chi or unki sarkaar ko jimmedaar tehraaya he
 SP president Akhilesh Yadav seems to be constantly failing in managing and saving his father Mulayam Singh's political legacy
 ek ke baad ek lagaataar teen chunaav main sapa ko karaari haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 Not only this, Rajput leaders are leaving Akhilesh one by one
 somvaar ko purv pradhanmantri chandrashekhar ke bete niraj shekhar ne rajyasabha ke saath hi saath samaajawaadee party se bhi istipha de diya
 Neeraj Shekhar was considered very close to Akhilesh Yadav
 bataa den ki samaajawaadee party ko uttar pradesh main satta kii bulandi tak pahunchane main yadav or musalamaanon ke saath-saath rajput samudaay ke netaaon kii bhi ahm bhoomika rahi he
 The Rajput community was once considered to be the original votebank of the SP
 purvanchal se lekar pashchim upi tak ke rajput netaa sapa kii saikil par savaar the
 From Amar Singh to Raghuraj Pratap Singh and Brij Bhushan Sharan Singh were seen playing political innings
 uttar pradesh kii satta se 2002 main rajnath singh ke hatane ke baad rajputon kii pehali pansad sapa ban gai thi
 There was participation of Rajput community from sp's national organization to district organization
 2003 main mulaayam singh yadav kii sarkaar banane main rajput netaaon ne mukhya kirdaar nibhaayaa tha
 This is the reason why Mulayam made Rajputs a part of Yadav and Muslims in his power
 itnaa hi nahin amar singh jaise rajput netaa sapa main ahm faisle liya karte the
 Once upon a time, at the behest of Amar Singh, Mulayam Singh showed Azam Khan a way out of the party
 mulaayam singh yadav ne 2012 main apni raajnneetik viraasat akhilesh yadav ko saunpi
 After this, the caste equation created by Mulayam began to disintegrate
 haalanki ye vahi daur tha jab bijepi dobaaraa se majboot honi shuru hui thi
 Since the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, the process of Rajput leaders leaving the SP in the state has started the same
 dilachasp baat yah he ki sapa kaa saath chhodane vaale zyaadaatar netaaon ne bijepi kaa daaman thama he
 Neeraj Shekhar, son of former Prime Minister Chandrasekhar, resigned from SP on Monday
 niraj shekhar ab apni raajnneetik pari bijepi ke saath shuru karne ja rahe hai
 In this Lok Sabha election, Neeraj Shekhar was angry due to Ballia not being given a ticket
 niraj shekhar sapa kaa saath chhodane vaale iklaute rajput netaa nahin he
 These lists are very long, including the names of Mayankeshwar Sharan Singh, Raj Kishore Singh, Brij Bhushan Singh, Raja Aridaman Singh, Kritivardhan Singh, Anand Singh, Akshay Pratap Singh and Yashwant Singh
 sapa main amar singh kii ek samay tuuti bolti thi, lekin shivpal or akhilesh ke bich hui varchasv kii jang ke baad unhen party se baahar kaa rasta dikhaa diya gaya
 Apart from this, Raghuraj Pratap Singh (raja Bhaiya) has not been a member of SP, but was considered a staunch supporter
 unhone rajyasabha ke chunaav main sapa ke khilaaf bagawati rukh akhriyaar kar liya
 Raja Bhaiya has formed his political party
 america ke raashtrapati baraak obama ne somvaar ko kaha ki orlando ke samalangik club main 49 logon kii hatya karne vaala bandookdhaari 'internet par prasaarit charampanth se sambandhi jaankariyon' se prerit tha, lekin uske iesas kii vyapak sajeesh kaa hissaa hone ke sanket nahin hai
 Obama described it as a clear example of 'home-grown terrorism'
 jaanch main juty he epabiaiamerica khufia agency epabiai ke saath subah sankshipt baithak ke baad obama ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, 'ek baat jo kahi ja sakati he wo ye ki iseatankwaadi jaanchake taur par liya ja rahaa he
 The attacker appears to have been inspired by various extremism-related information circulating on the Internet
 ' unhone bataaya ki philhal chaanbin or padtaal kii ja rahi he taaki epabiai hatyare ke hamalaa karne ke faisle ke bare main behatar samaj bana sake
 The 'homegrown' terrorist was a 'terrorist' Orlando attacker himself
 The FBI has said that the Orlando attacker was a radical terrorist in Omar Matinaghar, who had spread fanaticism on the Internet
 epabiai ne kaha ki vah islamic state aatankwaadi samooh sahit kisi bhi videshi vaishvik aatankwaadi network kaa sadsy nahin tha
 FBI Director James Comey said at a press conference in Washington, "there are no indications so far that we can say that the conspiracy for this firing was hatched by outside elements and we have to There is also no indication that he (the attacker) was a member of any terrorist network
 ' matin ke 50 logon ko maarane or 53 anya ko ghayal karne kii ghatana ke ek din baad kome ne kaha ki ab tak hui jaanch se yah pataa chalaa he ki is vakt yah puri tarah se spasht nahin he ki vah kisi aatankwaadi sanghathan kaa samarthan karnaa chahta tha
 Father said, would hand him over to the police
 Meanwhile, Matin's father said that if he got even a percentage of what his son was plotting, he would have handed over his son to the police and the FBI
 
 bete kii karatuut ke liye maangi maafisiddiqui mir matin ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, 'main ek baar phir maafee maangana chahta hum
 This is very sad news for all American people today
 main aape se baahar ho gaya hum
 If i had any idea that my son would commit such a crime, i would have dealt with it myself and called the FBI or local law enforcement
 ' There has been a terrorist attack in Shopian in Jammu and Kashmir
 aatankiyon ne shopiyaan ke esaspi kii gaadi par hamalaa kiya he
 No damage is reported in this attack
 bataa den ki shanivaar kii subah aatankiyon ne jammu kashmir main shopiyaan ke hajipura esaspi or edinshnal espi kii gaadi par hamalaa kiya
 However, the police immediately opened fire on those terrorists
 police kii javaabi firing ke baad aatanki maukey se faraar ho gaye
 Terrorist attacks have intensified in Kashmir
 aapako bataa den ki 10 march ko srinagar main ek police thane main grenade se hamalaa kiya gaya tha
 Two policemen were injured in this attack
 vahiin 11 march ko aatankiyon ke dwaara pidipi vidhayak majid paddar ke ghar par bhi grenade se hamalaa kiya gaya tha
 However, during this time when the attack took place, Majeed was not at home
 is hamale ke baad sena nejammu-kashmirake anantnag jile main teen aatankiyon ko maar giraaya tha
 In South Africa, medical student Kajal Lutchmerian won the title of Miss India World Wide 2010 in a spectacular ceremony held here
 durban ke antarrashtriya sammelan sthal main yojit bhavy kaarykram main britain kii niharika rayjada pehali ranor ap or surinam kii cher marchand tisare sthaan par raheen
 Beauties of Indian origin living in 25 countries participated in this competition
 lutchameriun ke liye yah puraskaar paanaa ek vishesh mauka rahaa kyonki thik 150 saal pehle dakshin africa ke ganne ke kheton main kaam karne ke liye bhartiya majdoor vahaan pahunche the or dakshin africa is varsh uske purvajon ke yahaan pahunchane kii 150veen vasharganth manaa rahaa he
 Lüchmerian will represent India globally for the next one year
 puraskaar jeetne ke baad lutchameriun ne pitiai se kaha ki vah is khitaab kaa istemaal dakshin africa ke garib samudaayon main echivi-aids ke khilaaf abhiyaan shuru karne main karengi
 She has been doing this work for the last five years
 unhone kaha, ‘main bahut khush hum
 i was able to bring this crown home
 main samajhati hum ki is baar dakshin africa kii baari thi
 i grew up here on a sugarcane farm in Tongaat and i think it is important that our ancestors came here 150 years ago so that this town and this country could be ours
 ’ Vaishnavism is the community of those who consider Lord Vishnu as God
 vaishnav dharm yaa vaishnav sampradaay kaa pracheen naam bhagwat dharm yaa pancharaatr mat he
 The principal worshiper of this sect is the god Vasudeva, who, by virtue of knowledge, power, strength, semen, opulence and glory - these 6: qualities are called God or 'bhagavata' and worshipers of the Bhagavata are called Bhagavata
 vaishnav ke bahut se up sampradaay hai
 Such as: Bairagi, Das, Ramananda, Vallabh, Nimbark, Madhva, Radhavallabh, Sakhi and Gaudiya
 vaishnav kaa mularoop aditya yaa surya dev kii aradhana main miltaa he
 Important facts related to Vaishnava religion or sect: (1) General information about Vaishnavism is available from Upanishads
 iskaa vikaas bhagavat dharm se hua he
 (2) The originator of the Vaishnava religion was Krishna, who belonged to the Vrishika clan and whose residence was Mathura
 (3)krishna kaa sabase pehle ullekh chhandogya upanishad main devaki ke bete or angiras ke shishy ke rup main hua

 (ii)iske sanyasi sir mundakar chotii rakhte hai

 However, the question remains in most people whether fruit juice is more beneficial or vegetable juice
 iskaa jawaab he- aapako apane zeus ke seven main 90 / 10 ke niyam kaa paalan karnaa chahie
 That is, your juice should have 90 percent vegetables and 10 percent fruits
 iske peeche vajah ye he ki falon main fructose ke rup main zyada natural sugar hoti he
 Whether it is juice or dried fruit, both of them have high sugar because they are concentrated
 falon ke zeus main subjiyon ke zeus ke mukaable sugar kii maatra zyada hoti he
 When you extract fruit juice, you are removing the fiber part of it
 fibre sugar relies ko dhimaa karata he lekin fibre nikal jane se sugar relies zyada hota he or insulin kaa str bad jaataa he
 Even though this sugar is natural, but also a high amount of natural sugar in the juice can affect insulin levels
 isse bhukh bad jaati he or vajan badhane jaisi chijen hone lagati hai
 That is why you should include only 10 percent sweet fruits and vegetables in your juice
 is niyam ke apwaad sirf neembu or khattey fal hai jinamein natural sugar kii maatra kam hoti he or khun main blad insulin kii maatra nahin badhati he

 sabase acha tarika ye he ki aap smudi yaa milkshek, nuts, oats or kuch taaje falon kaa seven ek saath karen
